-- Table structure for table `account`

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `account` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `stud_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `payment_date` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `money_receipt_no` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `amount_payable` double NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `amount_paid` double NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `amount_due` double NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `payment_status` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `received_by` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('active','inactive') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
  `meta_keywords` text NOT NULL,
  `meta_description` text NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime NOT NULL,
  `modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `admissioninfo_account_FK` (`stud_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;

-- Table structure for table `admission_info`

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `admission_info` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `stud_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `stud_name` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `course_name` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `money_receipt_no` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `admission_date` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `batch_no` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `batch_day` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('active','inactive') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
  `meta_keywords` text NOT NULL,
  `meta_description` text NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime NOT NULL,
  `modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `stud_id` (`stud_id`),
  KEY `course_admissioninfo_FK` (`course_name`),
  KEY `batch_no` (`batch_no`),
  KEY `batch_day` (`batch_day`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 ROW_FORMAT=COMPACT AUTO_INCREMENT=9 ;

-- Table structure for table `blog_posts`

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blog_posts` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `date` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `content` longtext NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `excerpt` text,
  `status` varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'published',
  `comment_status` varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'open',
  `ping_status` varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'open',
  `password` varchar(20) DEFAULT '',
  `uri` varchar(200) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `modified` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `comment_count` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `tags` text,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `uri` (`uri`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `media_cat`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `media_cat` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `media_cat` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `media_type` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('active','inactive') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
  `meta_keywords` text NOT NULL,
  `meta_description` text NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `media_cat` (`media_cat`),
  KEY `mediatype_mediacat_FK` (`media_type`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 ROW_FORMAT=COMPACT AUTO_INCREMENT=21 ;

  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `version` int(10) DEFAULT '0',
  `status` varchar(200) DEFAULT 'on',

) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC AUTO_INCREMENT=8 ;

  `type` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `size` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('active','inactive') NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime NOT NULL,
  `modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=9 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `page_contents`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `page_contents` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `page_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `language` varchar(250) DEFAULT NULL,
  `keywords` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `date` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `title` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `excerpt` text,
  `content` longtext NOT NULL,
  `uri` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `tags` text,
  `view` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `modified` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `password` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` varchar(200) DEFAULT 'published',
  `type` varchar(250) DEFAULT NULL,
  `target` varchar(250) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `uri` (`uri`),
  KEY `language` (`language`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC AUTO_INCREMENT=13 ;

-- Dumping data for table `page_contents`
--

-- Table structure for table `pages`

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `pages` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `level` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `lft` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `rgt` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `scope` int(11) DEFAULT '1',
  `title` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `type` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `target` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC AUTO_INCREMENT=7 ;

-- Table structure for table `personal_info`

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `personal_info` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `stud_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `father_name` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `mother_name` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `mailing_address` text NOT NULL,
  `permanent_address` text NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `cell_no` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `picture` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `size` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `type` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('active','inactive') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
  `meta_keywords` text NOT NULL,
  `meta_description` text NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime NOT NULL,
  `modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `stud_id` (`stud_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=10 ;

-- Table structure for table `roles`

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `roles` (
  `id` int(11) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `description` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uniq_name` (`name`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `semisters`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `semisters` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `stud_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `course_name` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `semister_no` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `semister_course_details` text NOT NULL,
  `admission_fees` double NOT NULL,
  `fees_per_module` double NOT NULL,
  `modules_in_semister` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `vat` double NOT NULL,
  `discount` double NOT NULL,
  `semister_total_fees` double NOT NULL,
  `amount_payable` double NOT NULL,
  `amount_paid` double NOT NULL,
  `amount_due` double NOT NULL,
  `payment_date` date NOT NULL,
  `money_receipt_no` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `amount_received_by` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('active','inactive') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
  `meta_keywords` text NOT NULL,
  `meta_description` text NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime NOT NULL,
  `modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `semisters_course_FK` (`course_name`),
  KEY `semester_no` (`semister_no`),
  KEY `stud_id` (`stud_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 ROW_FORMAT=COMPACT AUTO_INCREMENT=2 ;

--
-- Dumping data for table `semisters`
--

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `users`
--

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `users` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `email` varchar(200) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `username` varchar(200) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `password` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `logins` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `homepage` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `first_name` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_name` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `registered_on` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_login` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uniq_username` (`username`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uniq_email` (`email`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=COMPACT AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;

) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=5 ;

-- Constraints for dumped tables

--
-- Constraints for table `about`
--

  ADD CONSTRAINT `abouttype_aboutus_FK` FOREIGN KEY (`about_type`) REFERENCES `about_type` (`about_type`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE CASCADE;

-- Constraints for table `acca_media`
--

  ADD CONSTRAINT `accamedia_mediacat_FK` FOREIGN KEY (`media_cat`) REFERENCES `media_cat` (`media_cat`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  ADD CONSTRAINT `mediatype_accamedia_FK` FOREIGN KEY (`media_type`) REFERENCES `media_type` (`media_type`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE CASCADE;
